class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">葛开英、葛玲仁、葛志慧、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">戈觉平、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">格桑梅朵（藏）、格桑秀郎（藏）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">革命（哈萨克）、革振华、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">根托（藏）、根珠（藏）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">耿宜敏、耿引凤、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">更敦扎巴（藏）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">宫宝美、宫文义、宫正、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">公华、公丕启、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">巩进军</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">贡嘎（藏）、贡觉尼玛（藏）、贡却才培（藏）、贡却卓玛（藏）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">龚圣亮</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">古丽米拉•艾明（维吾尔）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">谷明龙、谷秀华、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">官忠基、</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">关振林、桂敏海、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">郭成茹、郭春该、郭洪伟、郭宏英、郭金丹、郭泉、郭延达、郭秀云、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">果然、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">高福志：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黑龙江省巴彦县法轮功学员。高福志<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日在家中被巴彦县兴华派出所警察绑架。依兰县法院定于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日非法庭审高福志。高福志聘请的律师起诉巴彦公检法人员迫害高福志，巴彦公检法人员威胁高福志，让其辞退律师、撤销对他们的起诉，说可以对高福志从轻处理，否则对高福志重判。高福志辞退了律师。结果<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日开庭时，没有律师到庭为高福志辩护。法院最近宣布对高福志非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。目前高福志依然关押在依兰县看守所。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">高国香：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东省德州市陵城区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">74</span>岁。自<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月中共迫害法轮功以来，高国香屡遭迫害。她曾被抓捕九次、拘禁关押共九次（关押四次、拘禁五次）、骚扰三次、抄家七次、勒索三万二千六百余元，劳教迫害一次，判刑一次。她还经历过：照相、抽血、按手印、签字、打耳光、拽头发、罚跪、脚踢、辱骂、逼看污蔑法轮功的录像、精神洗脑、逼迫写所谓“三书”、奴役等多种形式迫害，给老人精神身体及家人造成无法弥补的伤害。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，她和法轮功学员董娟，在德城区所辖赵虎乡镇集市上法轮功资料时，被抓捕，被关押在德州看守所，并被抄家，被抄走法轮功经书等。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，高国香老太太被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，罚款二万元。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">高亨柏：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东省青岛市平度市法轮功学员。山东平度市法院于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日将法轮功学员高亨柏判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年有期徒刑。山东省青岛法院<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月又高亨柏上诉案维持原判。高亨柏住在山东平度市南村镇（原兰底镇）小阵村。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，高亨柏在兰底镇集市上向老百姓免费赠送<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年新年台历，宣传法轮大法，被不明真相的人恶告。随后兰底派出所警察绑架了高亨柏，当天上午，兰底派出所警察到高亨柏家非法抄家。后被关押在平度市门村看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">高建君：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">江苏省连云港市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，连云港市海州区公安分局抓捕了法轮功学员刘玉萍、邵世玲、那仁志、熊成霞、周翠萍、马宝玲、高建君、王艾芝、汪宝玉、小周女士、乔老太等十一人。所有人家中都被非法抄了家，警察劫走家中的电脑、手机、光盘、<span lang="EN-US">U</span>盘、电器、钱财、书籍等私人物品。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，高建君被开庭，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">高锦标</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：男，河南省新密市公民，<span lang="EN-US">1989</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日出生。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，因言获罪被行政拘留，随后又转为刑事拘留，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，被正式逮捕。罪名是寻衅滋事。后法院以其在<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月至<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月在海外网站推特上“大量散布反对党和国家以及政府的言论、图片和视频”，严重损害国家形象和国家利益，于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日将高锦标判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。高锦标不服上诉，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，二审又维持原判。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">高俊</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：辽宁省鞍山市人，法轮功信仰者。因信仰、宣传法轮功，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日晚在高俊的七岭子家中，高俊、张永宝二人被辽阳公安局警察跟踪绑架、构陷，后经辽阳县法院三次庭审，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日二人被一审以犯“邪教罪”分别冤判有期徒刑。其中，高俊被重判<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万元，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，其不服已提起上诉。张永宝被冤判<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年，处罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; lang="EN-US">28</span>日被当地警察绑架。高立娟遭构陷的案卷两次被检察院退回，办案单位大港胜利派出所及大港国继续罗列罪名，又把高立娟起诉到天津滨海新区法院，意欲高立娟重判<span lang="EN-US">12</span>到<span lang="EN-US">14</span>年徒刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">高连红：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东省高密市拒城河社区法轮功学员。<span minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">60</span>多岁，山东省青岛市城阳区流亭赵村人，法轮功学员。因信仰法轮功而被青岛市当局多次绑架迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日下午，高文淑和丈夫邵承洛在夏庄镇发法轮功宣传材料时，被当地治安人员告发，当场即被夏庄派出所警方以涉“邪教罪”抓走，其家被查抄四次，并且警方在没有出具任何凭据的情况下，劫走家里二万元现金及许多物品。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，城阳区法院在城阳看守所内设法庭，高文淑和她的丈夫均被非法庭审，当庭未予宣判。之后，高文淑的家人为她聘请了律师，但律师向法官提出再次庭审要求时遭到拒绝。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，其夫妇二人被山东青岛城阳区法院以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”分别宣判，其被重判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，其丈夫被重判<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年。两人不服，均已提出上诉。目前被关押在青岛市城阳看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: minor-fareast;">高维平：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2018</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">52</span>岁、北京市东城区女法轮功学员、原中国新闻社研究部采编，<span lang="EN-US">1992</span>年修炼法轮法。<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>年中国大水灾，她默默拿出<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，被侨办、中新社非法处分，扣发工资，无故开除，失去经济来源，并被迫与丈夫离婚，独身一人生活。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，高维平<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日在北京王府井新华书店将真相书签放入书内，被书店经理诬告，后被东城区东方广场派出所数名警察绑架。东方广场派出所成立一个近十人的所谓“案件小组”，将高维平构陷到东城检察院。被构陷所谓“破坏法律实施<span lang="EN-US">300</span>条”，被关押在东城区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，法轮功学员高维平被东城区法院非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，并勒索罚款八千元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: minor-fareast;">四川泸州市合江县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年七十五岁。高贤英曾被非刑两次，一次<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，一次<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日被四川泸州市合江县法院高显英被判<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，处罚金七千。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东潍坊市昌邑市法轮功学员，在中共对法轮功持续至今近<span lang="EN-US">20</span>年的迫害中，被迫流离失所多年，落脚在聊城市东昌府区。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日与法轮功学员黄焕芝，在散发真相资料时，被李海务派出所警察抓捕，关押在聊城市看守所。于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日高小平被山东聊城法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年零<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，黄焕芝被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。两名善良妇女现已在山东女子监狱服刑。高小平刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">高智晟：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> 1964</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日出生，陕西省榆林市佳县人，著名维权律师。<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年起，开始替弱势群体维权打官司，曾处理过多宗民间维权案件；自<span lang="EN-US">2004</span>年底起，开始多次上书中共当局高层，要求改变对法轮功等群体的非法处理手段，并参与对法轮功学员器官遭当局活摘指控的调查；<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，与妻子公开宣布退出中国共产党；因其勇于于为当局认定的敏感性案件（注：含法轮功信仰者、地下基督教徒以及与官员发生纠纷的底层农民和私营企业家）辩护，故而曾多次受到中共官方机构或组织（<span lang="EN-US">610</span>办公室）黑社会手段的严重骚扰和打击报复；<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，其执业执照被当局吊销，随后被秘密绑架并遭到约<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个月的酷刑。<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，被北京市第一中级法院以“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，缓刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年；<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日起其与外界失联，至<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月才被当局释放返京；后因其接受了美联社采访，遂被再次与外界失联，直至<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，其亲友才从新华社报导中得知，其缓刑已被北京法院撤销，须继续服刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>个月，至<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日刑满出狱，此前在新疆维吾尔自治区沙雅监狱服刑。出狱后高智晟仍被严密监控，且不让治牙看病，致其因长期在狱中遭受酷刑折磨和被单独囚禁，迄今仍牙齿松动，身体健康欠佳；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，其在陕北老家秘密撰写的新书《<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年，起来中国》在台湾正式印刷出售，因该书涉及中共当局对其长期绑架、囚禁和施以酷刑等，以及他从信仰角度看中共<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年将会灭亡和对<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年后的中国未来宪政民主化展望等三大内容，遂令当局十分恐惧、恼怒，对其监控愈加严密。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月中旬在老家失踪，后获知被当局控制带回北京关押。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">葛开英：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">上海维权人士。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日上午，葛开英被上海警察和其他多人在北京街道上绑架，押回上海铐往黄浦区看守所刑事拘留。这是继去年将葛开英无理由关押于黑监狱十多天折磨以及其他数十次限制人身自由的政府恐怖主义罪行外，黄浦区政府伙同公安部门犯下的又一罪行。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">葛玲仁</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：辽宁盘锦市<span lang="EN-US">74</span>岁女法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日早上大约九点多在早市买菜时，葛玲仁被人诬告， 渤海派出所给家人打电话配合他抄家，在家人未配合的情况下把葛玲仁带回家抢走钥匙开门抄家，抄走电脑、书籍、八百多元钱。大约晚上八点多钟渤海派出所所长张军及办案责任人韩世龙，带葛玲仁到盘锦市中心医院体检，之后送到拘留所，拘留所拒收，血压高<span lang="EN-US">(170/100)</span>。在老人血压高拘留所拒收的情况下第二次带老人体检。最后在老人一天食水未进，身体虚弱的情况下，不顾老人安危强行把老人抱上车送到盘锦市看守所，在看守所又拒收的情况下，又第三次到盘锦辽河油田第二医院体检，在根本没检查身体的情况下，弄了个假证明后强行送到盘锦市看守所非法关押迫害。<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日上午九点通知家属，盘锦市兴隆台区人民检察院批捕，一周后案卷返回渤海派出所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">北京市丰台区岳各庄的维权残疾人。住北京丰台区魏家村南<span lang="EN-US">20</span>号院<span lang="EN-US">1</span>号楼门<span lang="EN-US">2</span>门<span lang="EN-US">1305</span>室。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，葛志慧和同区石榴庄东街<span lang="EN-US">195</span>号的被强拆人李美青，到达中央扫黑除恶督导组驻地反映政府的黑社会化强拆，结果在督导组驻地的门口，遭到丰台区副区长带队的维稳人员的阻截，求见扫黑除恶督导组未果。但是，没隔多久，葛志慧竟遭刑事拘留。罪名是寻衅滋事。关押在丰台看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">戈觉平</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：江苏苏州维权人士。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日戈觉平（网络名称：奔博）被苏州市公安局直属分局以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”指定居所监视居住。戈觉平（奔博）、陆国英夫妇是癌症病患者，尤其是戈觉平，需要长期服中药，其身体状况令人担忧。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">戈觉平至<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月已被超期羁押近两年，狱中身体状况不佳，一直高血压，现在每天要吃五颗降压药，平时都躺着休息。日前又传出其在看守所原病处有发炎、化脓症状，之前家属和律师曾多次向看守所提出取保申请，却一直未获批准。其妻陆国英反映，丈夫以前得过癌症，后做手术治愈，但需长期服中药，而看守所根本不具备熬药的条件，她现在非常担心丈夫的身体状况。希望看守所方面能尽快批准他的取保申请。到<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月仍未开庭。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，苏州中院判处戈觉平煽动颠覆罪<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月有期徒刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">格桑梅朵：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">西藏拉萨一小学女教师。格桑梅朵是第一位可以被知道的因翻墙而遭中共当局强迫失踪的藏人。据了解，格桑梅朵曾在<span lang="EN-US">Facebook</span>上转发外媒 《自由亚洲电台》和《挪威西藏之声》中文部有关藏区的新闻报道，以促进使用<span lang="EN-US">Facebook</span>的中国网友，特别是她的汉族朋友们了解西藏问题的真相。梅朵非常了解西藏的历史和现实。格桑梅朵翻墙转发外媒西藏新闻一事被发现后，当局开始对她进行迫害，她所在的小学将梅朵开除，梅朵继而于<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年遭到当局强迫失踪，至今已下落不明<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。现获悉，格桑梅朵被以“泄露国家秘密”定罪，关押地点不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">格桑秀郎（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">出生不详，西藏那曲地区比如县达木寺僧人。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日在拉萨市被拉萨警方拘捕，后一直被秘密关押，直至<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日获知，其被拉萨市中级法院以“带领民众集会”罪名判处<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年有期徒刑。目前被关押在西藏拉萨的扎其监狱。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">革命（哈萨克）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">他与叶尔波里（哈萨克）都是新疆伊犁州阿尔泰地区哈巴河县哈萨克族人，自由职业者，伊斯兰教信仰者，哈萨克族人权捍卫者。由于没有办理信教许可证（即未到当地政府部门申请批准），坚持自行做祷告，并经常到清真寺，因此于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5-6</span>月被抓捕，后于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月上旬分别被阿尔泰地区哈巴河县法院以“从事非法宗教活动罪”判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。据一位哈萨克同乡称，因他们都无正式职业，平时靠打散工或装修房子度日，二人家庭都十分贫困。被捕后，当地公安不准家属聘请律师，也拒绝向家属出示判决书。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5-6</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">革振华：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">63</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">岁，黑龙江省哈尔滨市阿城区人，原阿城区低压电器厂职工，法轮功学员。因信仰法轮功，<span lang="EN-US">2002</span>年曾被哈尔滨市阿城市公安局非法劳教<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。在哈尔滨市长林子劳教所期间，经常遭到警察和犯人的毒打，被强迫长时间坐小板凳等。因劳教所环境恶劣，他身上长满了疥疮，疼痛难忍。每天还要强迫他做十几个小时的苦役，完不成任务就罚站。其左肋骨曾被警察和犯人打断两根，但仍不放过他，逼他出工干活，一天也不许休息。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日凌晨，他在哈尔滨市尚志市亮河镇挂条幅、散发法轮功宣传资料时，被当地警方闻讯赶来围捕、绑架，后被关押在尚志市看守所。与其一起的法轮功学员菽坤和王翠娥也遭抓捕，至今未归。因长期不知革振华的消息，其妻经多方打听，直至<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月才知道丈夫革振华已被哈尔滨市尚志市法院以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”枉法冤判<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年。据悉，革振华不服，提起上诉，但二审仍维持原判。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。目前服刑当地不明。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">根托（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">四川甘孜藏区炉霍县人，藏族人权捍卫者。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，在西藏康区炉霍县境内发生大规模和平示威活动后，中共军警釆取武力镇压，导致云丹为首的多名藏人被开枪打死或打伤，上百人遭捕。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日中共当局对<span lang="EN-US">16</span>名遭捕的藏人进行判决，其中一名藏人被判终身监禁，另有多人遭<span lang="EN-US">1</span>至<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年不等的有期徒刑。这<span lang="EN-US">16</span>名被判藏人中，已确切得知的有<span lang="EN-US">10</span>名藏人具体情况，其中：根托，现年<span lang="EN-US">20</span>多岁，被判<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年徒刑，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">根珠（藏）</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：四川甘孜藏区炉霍县人，藏族人权捍卫者。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，在西藏康区炉霍县境内发生大规模和平示威活动后，中共军警釆取武力镇压，导致云丹为首的多名藏人被开枪打死或打伤，上百人遭捕。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日中共当局对<span lang="EN-US">16</span>名遭捕的藏人进行判决，其中一名藏人被判终身监禁，另有多人遭<span lang="EN-US">1</span>至<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年不等的有期徒刑。这<span lang="EN-US">16</span>名被判藏人中，已确切得知的有<span lang="EN-US">10</span>名藏人具体情况，其中：根珠，现年<span lang="EN-US">30</span>多岁，被判<span lang="EN-US">11</span>年徒刑，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">耿宜敏：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">安徽阜南县基督教堂 堂委会主任。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日中共当局强拆了安徽阜南县基督教堂，被强拆的安徽阜南县基督教堂可容纳<span lang="EN-US">3000</span>多人并在礼拜，聚会时几乎座无虚席。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日下午，在没有任何合法的文件通知下遭到强拆，甚至教堂财物尽毁，来不及搬出。堂委会主任耿宜敏、牧师孙永耀于<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日下午<span lang="EN-US">3</span>点被以“涉嫌聚众扰乱社会秩序罪”刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">耿引凤</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：女，<span lang="EN-US">79</span>岁，江苏省靖江市人，法轮功信仰者，良心犯。因信法轮功而长期遭当地<span lang="EN-US">610</span>办公室及当地警方监控和迫害，曾多次被警察非法抓捕关押。一次她被关在派出所里强制 “转化”，她就跟警察讲真相，结果却被绑吊在门栏上面一天一夜，遭警方打耳光、用脚踢、撞门框子等，还不让睡觉，不给饭吃和喝水。之后，她很快被枉法判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。狱中遭非人待遇，因抵制被洗脑转化，曾被倒吊三天三夜，直至昏死。出狱后，<a href="https://www.blogger.com/null" name="_Hlk512566287"><span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日</a>，在南京江宁天泽苑公寓的家中，其又被警方抓走，并关押在靖江公安局看守所<span lang="EN-US">16</span>天。同年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，靖江市警方再次将其从南京家中劫持到靖江法院，并对她进行非法开庭。当时没有宣判结果，非法关押<span lang="EN-US">20</span>天后又放回家。收监逮捕后，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日其被江苏省泰州市靖江市法院开庭受审，被以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”再次诬判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。但据称，江苏省泰州市看守所拒绝收押耿引凤老人。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">更敦扎巴（藏）</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：现年<span lang="EN-US">40</span>岁，四川省阿坝羌族藏族自治州若尔盖县唐克镇索藏村人，索克藏寺续部学院资深僧人和寺院办公室职员。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日夜里在自己僧舍里突遭一批不属于当地警方的国保警察野蛮抓捕。抓捕时，不仅没有说明理由，而且还使用暴力，用手铐铐住双手，用枪顶住脸部。此后长期失联，官方拒绝透露其被捕原因、关押地点及其身体状况等信息。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，其被四川阿坝羌族藏族自治州黑水县法院以“煽动分裂国家”、“非法联系境外”罪判处徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，关押地点不详。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">宫宝美：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">安徽省蚌埠市法轮功学员。安徽省宿州市灵璧县<span lang="EN-US">610</span>及国保大队人员、蚌埠市<span lang="EN-US">610</span>及国保大队人员共十几人，在<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日上午<span lang="EN-US">9</span>点多，闯入家在蚌埠市禹会区一所居民楼法轮功学员宫宝美家，强行搜查，掠去几万元现金，据目击者说，打印机器及各种真相资料，装有几车运走。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，宫宝美被蚌埠市灵璧县法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">宫文义：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">哈尔滨市道外区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日哈尔滨市松北区公安分局绑架了宫文义等<span lang="EN-US">13</span>名法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，其他<span lang="EN-US">12</span>名法轮功学员被松北区检察院起诉。宫文义因身体原因保外回家，检察院称另案处理。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，宫文义在哈尔滨市江北住处，警察再次抓捕，并被抄家。后被在哈市第一看守所关押。后宫文义于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日被哈市道外区法院秘密开庭并判刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日被押送哈市呼兰监狱。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">宫正：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">上海维权人士。宫敏赓、宫正兄弟俩于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日在上海南京路步行街撒传单时被带进派出所。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，兄弟俩人同时被上海市公安局黄浦分局以“寻衅滋事罪”为名刑事拘留。哥哥宫敏赓被刑事拘留一个月，于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日获释。弟弟宫正于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日被上海市公安局黄埔分局构陷“寻衅滋事罪”执行逮捕，现关押在上海市黄浦区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">1997</span>宫敏赓的公司合法经营，被上海市第一中级法院与黄浦区下属企业联手，用犯罪手段，抢劫掠夺了其所有的合法财产，至今已有<span lang="EN-US">22</span>年。尽管宫敏赓有足够的证据，但法院仍至今不归还其财产，也不立案。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年宫敏赓、宫正兄弟俩的父母留下来的房子，居住的权利被上海市第一中级法院枉法裁判剥夺。导致兄弟俩从<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年至今无家可归，到处流浪。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">公华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东省日照市法轮功学员，日照市裕华机械厂职工。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>、<span lang="EN-US">3</span>两日，日照市公安局东港分局国保警察先后抓捕了法轮功学员公华、孙平、屈正蓉等八位学员，关押在日照市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日公华被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">公丕启：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1955</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年出生，山东省青岛市人，前山东省预备役高炮师副参谋长、退休上校、正团职军官，法轮功信仰者，中国在押良心犯。自<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年信仰、锻炼法轮功以来，深受中共当局的打压逼迫；曾因其家人及其本人均锻炼法轮功之故而被迫提前“退休”，并遭多次威胁，被当局用开除“党籍”、撤销职务及工资待遇、收回住房、开除孩子学籍、投入监狱等方式胁迫其放弃修炼；<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，曾与妻子在家中被青岛市警方以邪教罪由拘捕，后其妻被枉法判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，其虽未被判刑，但被关押在部队接受洗脑再教育，其女儿在外上学也因此断绝了生活来源，无家可归；关押期间，因拒绝放弃信仰而被长期关小屋，遭受酷刑虐待，直至在经历了<span lang="EN-US">7</span>个半月的磨难之后才得以释放；因其坚持信仰不动摇，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，在去朋友家中串门之际再次被青岛市市北区警方以涉嫌“邪教罪”刑拘，家被查抄；同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，被转正式逮捕，并关押在青岛市即墨普东看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，其案被青岛市市北区法院在青岛市即墨普东看守所内正式开庭，同年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，被以“邪教罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金人民币<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元；其不服提起上诉，经青岛市中级法院二审裁决，依然维持原判，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日。目前服刑监狱不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">巩进军：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">曾因房屋遭遇强拆而上访多年，并屡遭截访，被遣返原籍；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，因长期滞留北京上访，遂被送至黑监狱马家楼关押，后又被遣返原籍，途中其一行四人（均为访民）因遭到黑保安的非人虐待且拘不让饮食，故而在其人身自由及安全被“黑保安”非法严重侵害的情况下被迫予以正当防卫，双方发生激烈冲突，引发刺死黑保安事件（警方称一死一伤）；案发后河北省饶阳县警方迅速将其抓捕刑拘，并被关押在河北省衡水市深州看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日被正式批捕；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日被河北省衡水市中院以“故意伤害罪”判处无期徒刑；据悉其在被审讯时曾遭严重酷刑，仅一天即被电击<span lang="EN-US">50</span>余次。目前在河北省某监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">贡嘎（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">出生年月不详，西藏自治区拉萨市林周县人，拉萨市林周县旁多乡藏民，职业不详，生态环境保护者，藏族人权捍卫者，中国在押政治犯。早从<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年起，中国政府就开始计划将在拉萨市林周县附近的矿区建设、实施“旁多水利枢纽工程”。因该工程要在两条交汇于林周县旁多乡的河流——热振河、旁多措河之上筑坝截水，故为确保顺利开工，相关政府部门就于<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年和<span lang="EN-US">2004</span>年两次召开藏民大会，郑告村民此工程是“中共中央的指令，若有藏人试图阻止施工，将以政治罪名进行拘捕”。随后几年，因有关部门迅速投入大量施工准备，不仅在当地做频繁测量、建桥及建路等工作，而且炸山挖石，大量采矿，随意排放污水，导致当地的自然生态环境出现严重毁坏，附近村民的民房出现裂痕及大面积农田被毁坏等现象。<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，因拉萨市林周县的“旁多水利枢纽工程”正式开工，当局随立即强迫旁多乡<span lang="EN-US">119</span>户（近<span lang="EN-US">700</span>名）藏民尽快整体搬迁。因当地藏民不愿搬迁，故而多次向政府部门提出投诉请求，但均毫无果效。<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月，遂被迫进行集体维权与和平请愿，以期能借此阻拦破坏生态环境的采矿项目。不料却遭到中共西藏当局的强烈打压。贡嘎、白玛等<span lang="EN-US">6</span>名藏族人权捍卫者因此遭拉萨市警方野蛮抓捕，自此失联。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年，贡嘎、白玛等一行<span lang="EN-US">6</span>人案分别被拉萨市法院以“试图分裂西藏，并组织领导了以保护环境为名的抗议活动”罪由秘判<span lang="EN-US">8</span>至<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年不等徒刑，其亦被判徒刑<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月。目前在西藏自治区第一监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">贡觉尼玛（藏）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1969</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年出生，四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州（以下简称阿坝州）若尔盖县人，西藏拉萨市哲蚌寺果芒学院经师，学者僧侣，中国在押良心犯。自幼成为僧侣，并长期进入西藏拉萨市哲蚌寺的果芒学院对佛教进修、研读；后因曾长期师从藏族著名佛学教师兰林仁波切（<span lang="EN-US">Lamrim<span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp; </span>Rinpoche</span>），成其身边主要弟子，加之自身对佛学严谨博学的治学态度，故而被哲蚌寺果芒学院确立为经师（即精通佛教经藏的僧人，又称佛教讲经诵经的师父）；<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，曾因藏区发生大规模以僧侣为主体，要求中共当局实现（或兑现）藏民族“自治独立”，并呼吁让达赖喇嘛回国返乡等政治诉求的抗议活动，<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，其所在寺庙约有<span lang="EN-US">350</span>名僧人亦积极参与其中，致使抗议活动态势迅速扩展到整个拉萨市区，以及四川、青海等藏区；针对此次抗议游行，中共西藏当局很快调拨大批持枪武警，因管控手段过于极端，遂导致双方发生对峙冲突，其间有不少僧人被抓捕，其余人等被送回寺庙严管看守；尽管此前其并未参加抗议游行活动，<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，其仍被拉萨市警方以涉嫌“抗议活动”抓走刑拘，自此失联；另有二名哲蚌寺好友、学者僧侣亦被一同抓捕；后其被拉萨市检察院正式批捕，理由是未能阻止哲蚌寺僧人举行大规模抗议行动；<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，在被长期关押<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年之久后，被拉萨市中级法院以不详罪名秘密重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">20</span>年，据悉，其辩护权遭剥夺，其狱中具体境况等信息不明。目前疑似在拉萨曲水监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">贡却才培（藏）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1970</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年出生，藏名<span lang="EN-US">Kunchok Tsephel Gopey Tsang</span>，甘肃省甘南藏族自治州玛曲县欧拉乡人，曾担任玛曲县藏文中学英语教师，并任玛曲县畜牧局公务员、藏语及藏族网络作家和琼迈藏语文学网编辑，中国在押政治犯、良心犯。<span lang="EN-US">1995</span>年曾因涉嫌政治活动而被拘押<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月，后无罪获释；<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年因在互联网上发表了与西藏<span lang="EN-US">3.14</span>事件有关的文章，同时向外界披露藏人在抗议事件中被镇压、军警抓捕寺院僧侣等消息，遂于<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日被从家中逮捕，并遭搜查，之后与外界失去联系；<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，被甘肃省甘南藏族自治州中级法院秘密审判，以“泄露国家机密罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">15</span>年。目前在甘肃省甘南自治州合作监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">贡却卓玛（藏）</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，四川省甘孜藏族羌族自治区州阿坝县藏人，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，因手中举着达赖喇嘛尊者的法相，在县城一处街道上和平游行，以此表达自己对达赖喇嘛尊者的崇敬，随立即被驻守在街道附近的中共警方拘捕。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">龚圣亮：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">基督教牧师，华南教案首犯。龚圣亮牧师是湖北省枣阳市人，华南教会（<span lang="EN-US">SCC</span>）的创始人和领袖，该教派是中国一个家庭教会团契，在几个省份有<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万名信徒。<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，龚圣亮在湖北省钟祥市被捕，同年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，他被湖北省荆门市中级法院裁定罪名成立，根据中国的反邪教法判处死刑。但由于国际压力，中国放弃了宗教罪名和死刑，并下令重新审判。中国湖北省高级法院后以事实不清、证据不足为由驳回了荆门市中级法院对基督教华南教会五名成员的死刑判决后，荆门市中级法院重新作出一审判决，把龚圣亮、徐福明、胡勇等三人改判无期徒刑，龚邦坤、李英改判<span lang="EN-US">15</span>年有期徒刑，原先在一审被判<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年和<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年徒刑的向凤屏和刘先知等四人获当庭释放。一些作证反对龚的人后来表示，他们遭到了残酷的刑讯逼供。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">古丽米拉•艾明（维吾尔）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1979</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年出生，新疆维吾尔自治区人，原任职乌鲁木齐政府机关工作人员，网络作家，中国在押政治犯、良心犯。<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年因在<span lang="EN-US">7</span>•<span lang="EN-US">5</span>事件发生时用手机短信向境外担任挪威维吾尔协会副秘书长的丈夫拜合提亚尔联系<span lang="EN-US">20</span>多次通报看到的情况，遂于<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日被新疆乌鲁木齐市警方逮捕，据称在拘留期间曾遭受酷刑虐待；<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，被新疆乌鲁木齐市中级人民法院以“分裂国家、泄露国家秘密和组织非法示威”罪判处无期徒刑。目前在乌鲁木齐水磨沟女子监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，刘希永、孙宝英、刘井龙的情况还不清楚。谷秀华刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; lang="EN-US">2018</span>年）<span lang="EN-US">66</span>岁，山东省平度市东阁办事处后巷子村人。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">关振林：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">甘肃省酒泉市法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">桂敏海：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">男，汉族，<span lang="EN-US">1964</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日出生，原籍中国宁波，<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年加入瑞典国籍，“巨流传媒有限公司”股东。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月及<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月的中共特工赴香港、泰国实施的“香港铜锣湾书店案”震惊世界，共绑架了<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人，分别是桂敏海、林荣基、吕波、张志平、李波。后此<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人都于<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年被中共逼迫在电视上认罪。桂敏海<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月中旬在央视称自己是为<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年前在宁波醉驾撞死人事件而潜返中国投案自首；<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，桂敏海又在电视镜头前承认自己非法偷运禁书进入大陆。后林荣基、吕波、张志平、李波相继被释放，唯有桂敏海遭扣押。中共当局一度声称桂敏海取保获释，实际上是仍遭秘密关押。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年被中共当局关押期间，中共称经其本人申请依法恢复中国国籍。宁波市中级法院于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日公开宣判，认定桂敏海犯为境外非法提供情报罪，判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">郭成茹：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">天津市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年五十四岁。郭成茹，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日被天津市河西区桃园派出所警察抓捕、非法关押、构陷。这是继郭成茹过去的六次被抓捕、十二年冤狱后的第七次被抓捕。从<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日到<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日这<span lang="EN-US">14</span>年间里，即从郭成茹三十五岁到四十九岁这段日子，她两次被非法劳教、两次被非法判刑、多次被非法拘留，累计<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年时间她是被囚禁在中共的看守所、劳教所、监狱中度过的。在对法轮功的灭绝政策下，她被多次野蛮灌食迫害，被酷刑吊铐折磨，被破坏中枢神经的药物迫害到一度失忆、失语、丧失认知、表达等能力，被警察包夹折磨到一度精神失常。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月份家人得知，郭成茹已被河西区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年、罚款五千元。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">郭春该</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：赵文静、黄金桔、吕月霞、郭春该及张迪<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">为涉</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河南省商丘巿宁陵县双庙村教会教案成员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日该教会一座兴建中的教堂，遭到数百名政府人员强拆，双方发生争执，教会物品被毁坏，信徒被打伤，数十人包括该<span lang="EN-US">5</span>名负责人被公安带走，后这<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人被拘留。他们被指涉嫌“寻衅滋事”及“非法拘禁”罪，<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日被县检察院正式逮捕。其中张迪是临近一教会的传道人，为协助该教会建教堂，而遭牵连得。目前，所有被捕者被羁押在宁陵县看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，该教会成立<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，信徒百多人，当局曾要求加入三自教会不遂。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">郭洪伟：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吉林省四平市铁东区人，人权捍卫者。原是吉林省白山市抚松县松江河发电厂职工，遭冤假错案报复陷害 ，入狱五年，逼迫上访十年至今未果。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月被构陷涉嫌“寻衅滋事”遭逮捕，<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日上午，郭洪伟、肖蕴玲被“敲诈吉林市公安局”一案在吉林省四平市公安局铁东区法院开庭审理。羁押于吉林省四平市看守所。原定于<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日开庭，当日家属接到通知要延期开庭，律师及家属寻人无果。后得知郭洪伟狱中遭遇酷刑，身体状况恶化被送医院。之后于<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日开庭，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日被吉林省四平市铁东区法院以“敲诈勒索罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">11</span>年，“寻衅滋事罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，最终执行有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">郭金丹：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">湖北省武汉市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日被几名国保警察勾结武汉市武昌区青菱乡张家湾派出所警察闯入法轮功学员郭金丹家中，在面对家人的质问，这些警察横不讲理，强行绑架了郭金丹，并扬言要把郭金丹作为重点，后得知已被转到武汉市第一看守所（武汉市东西湖二支沟）关押。今获知郭金丹被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">郭泉：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1968</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日出生，江苏省南京市人，原南京师范大学副教授、研究生导师，中国大陆新民党创始人及代理主席，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年曾因发表公开信要求中国进行宪政改革，宣布组建“中国新民党”，主张在中国实行多党制和军队国家化等，遭受到中共当局的打压，<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，被南京师范大学党委以违反宪法和教师法为由撤销其副教授职务，调任数据员；<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，又因撰文批评中国政府处理四川地震的方式不当而被拘押<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，再次因其在网上发表<span lang="EN-US">300</span>多篇名为《民主先声》的文章，其中涉及组成以宣传民主思想为目标的新民党，以及提出以不合作方式进行公民行动的蓝色运动倡议等内容，被南京市警方刑事拘留；<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，被江苏省宿迁市中级人民法院以“颠覆国家政权罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，刑满释放。此前在江苏省南京市浦口监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，原南京师范大学副教授、南京著名人权捍卫者郭泉因关注湖北武汉疫情，为疫区人民发声而遭中共当局抓捕，随即被刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，郭泉的母亲顾潇向媒体证实，郭泉本月中旬已经被南京检察院以“涉嫌煽动颠覆国家政权罪”批捕。南京警方指郭泉在网络上发表了国情及疫情等信息大<span lang="EN-US">500</span>篇文章，其中半数是在煽动民众。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal" style="background: white; mso-pagination: widow-orphan;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">郭宏英：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2018</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日是替母亲肖蕴苓、哥哥郭洪伟进京伸冤，而在“两会”期间被行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天的郭宏英女士获释的日子，郭宏英的八旬老父亲拖着病体到拘留所，结果眼睁睁看着女儿被四平市铁东区分局南四纬派出所的从截走，得到的是一张由行政拘留改为刑事拘留的家属通知书。郭宏英哥哥郭洪伟原是国企中层干部，因秉公管理得罪了某同事，被其在检察院的亲属报复构陷入狱五年，因此而走上了血泪上访路。上访过程中，为了维持生计，承包了个小诊所，经营刚有起色却遭到违约，且由公安违法参与民事纠纷，造成巨大的经济损失。真是福无双至祸不单行。痛上痛冤上冤把郭洪伟几尽逼上了绝路，逐渐悟出了信访是骗局，是在用时间杀害上访人，携年迈父母进京上访遭到地方政府以敲诈政府公安罪判刑<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年，其<span lang="EN-US">76</span>岁的老母亲也判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年。郭洪伟坐着轮椅，患高危三级高血压服刑，其母肖蕴苓多病缠身高龄服刑。服刑其间母子二人多次出现病危，当局不允许保外就医，有将母子二人冤死狱中的嫌疑。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日获悉：吉林四平公民郭宏英涉嫌寻衅滋事、妨害公务案四平市铁东区法院判决书已经下达，郭宏英被以寻衅滋事罪判决<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年有期徒刑，妨碍公务罪判决<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，执行<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年有期徒刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">郭延达：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辽宁省营口市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年六十一岁。被抓捕迫害前，在市内某大酒店当过厨师，因修炼法轮功，郭延达<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日被营口市站前区东桥派出所警察从家中抓捕。警察抄走郭延达家的私有财产：电脑、打印机、钱、汽车及一些物品。现在被关押在辽宁省沈阳市第一监狱第二监区。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日辽宁省营口市站前区法院对营口市法轮功学员郭延达等庭审，后得知郭延达被判刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"> </b><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">郭秀云：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">北京密云区不老屯镇雁洛村人，法轮功学员。因信法轮功，自<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年到<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年，曾先后三次被非法抓捕，其中两次被非法劳教。在劳教所，其虽受迫害，但仍坚持信仰，拒绝转化，拒写“三书”（保证书、决裂书、揭批书）。<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，其虽从山西省女子劳教所严管组被释放回家，但自此一直被当局视为重点“攻坚”对象，屡遭当地大队、<span lang="EN-US">610</span>、派出所、司法部门的上门骚扰、威胁、逼迫写“保证”及恐吓威胁，使其全家的正常生活受到严重干扰，家人感到巨大的压力和恐惧。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，中共开“两会”期间，郭秀云去亲友家路上，再次被不老屯派出所警方绑架，并被非法抄家，拿走电脑、打印机、法轮功真相币等私人物品，并被关押在北京市密云看守所。其关押期间，因受迫害而导致身体很差，在第一次被法庭庭审时，竟昏倒在地，家人多次要求放人遭拒。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，在没有通知家人的情况下，其被北京市密云区法院以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”秘密判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">果然： </span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1981</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日出生，北京市朝阳区人，陕西省西安市南郊大学城自由生意人，政治异见人士，中国在押政治犯（<span lang="EN-US">CPPC</span>编号：<span lang="EN-US">00709</span>）。近年来，因与友人经常在自己生意所在地聚会，自由讨论追求自由民主途径，被中共当局跟踪知晓，随于<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年二人被西安市长安区警方以涉嫌“颠覆国家政权罪”抓捕刑拘，关押在西安市南郊三爻村看守所；之后因当局控其欲与他人密谋推翻中共政府，其行为属于违法，随很快被西安市警方转正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，其案被陕西省西安市中级法院庭审，终被以“颠覆国家政权罪”一审重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">14</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年；另一人士亦被重判，但缺详情；据悉，因其平素做事隐秘，而当局对其审判亦不公开，故而对其入狱详情几乎鲜为人知，直至<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日陕西省渭南市中级法院在网上发布了一份“果然减刑刑事裁决书”才得知晓，渭南监狱鉴于其在狱中有悔过表现，积分较多，建议减刑，但渭南市中级法院却以“屡次严重违反监规被处分”为由拒不减刑，依旧刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年。目前在陕西省渭南监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 22.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">H.</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 22.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> <b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><o:p></o:p></b></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">哈布力（哈萨克）、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">哈哈尔麦<span lang="EN-US">.</span>阿合曼（</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">哈萨克）</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">哈里斯别克·巴班（哈）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">哈木拉提•吾甫尔（哈萨克）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">哈纳提别克•萨布尔别克（哈萨克）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">哈伊拉提别克•木合塔尔汗（哈萨克）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">海莱提•尼亚孜（维吾尔）、海米提·阿不都热合曼（维）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">郝福奎、郝劲松、郝明媚、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">韩爱珍、韩建海、韩良、韩猛、韩雪松、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">杭霞、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">何观娇、何华、何菊英、何林夏、何雪荣、何正琼、何宗旺、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">贺英、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黑伊特</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">洪桂连、洪柳、洪永忠、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">候敏玲、侯巧珍、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">胡光珍、胡功、胡石根、胡湘银、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">胡勇、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">胡友刚、胡占亭、胡志琴、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黄安阳、黄根吉、黄光玉、黄红萍、黄金桔、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黄兰凤</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、黄连、黄俊娟、黄琦、黄信、黄秀兰、黄雅珍、黄云敏、黄振超、黄志球、</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">哈布力（哈萨克）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">出生年月不详，新疆维吾尔自治区乌鲁木齐县人，哈萨克族，穆斯林，新疆乌鲁木齐县哈萨克族清真寺阿訇（即伊斯兰宗教事务主持人），伊斯兰宗教领袖。因近来中共当局加强了对新疆各民族在宗教信仰上的高压管控手段，哈萨克族人也不例外，此间，因哈布力是乌鲁木齐县哈萨克族群中知名宗教界领袖，影响力大，并与海外宗教性事务多有交流联系，随遭地方当局严厉打压；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年被乌鲁木齐县警方抓捕，后被乌鲁木齐县检察院正式批捕，控其“阅读及复印哈萨克斯坦国家宗教事务局的刊物”，违反了国家宗教问题的相关规定；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年被新疆乌鲁木齐县法院以不具名罪名判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年。据悉，当局对其如此重判是为了震慑新疆的哈萨克族人。目前服刑监狱不详。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">哈哈尔麦<span lang="EN-US">.</span>阿合曼：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1970</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日出生，新疆维吾尔自治区塔城地区沙湾县人，哈萨克族，前塔城地区东湾镇民族中学校长，前塔城地区沙湾县畜牧局党委书记，原塔城地区沙湾县第二中学校长，中国在押政治犯。早年曾就读于新疆塔城师范学院中专，<span lang="EN-US">1989</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月毕业后又在新疆教育学院政治系进修大专，并于<span lang="EN-US">1992</span>年毕业；曾常年在民族学校历任校长，<span lang="EN-US">1995</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月曾任新疆塔城地区东湾镇民族中学校长，<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年至被捕前，曾长期任塔城地区沙湾县第二中学校长等职；因工作敬业、成绩斐然，曾被多次被当地政府评为“先进个人”<span lang="EN-US">/</span>“双文明先进个人”；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，突然被沙湾县警方以不知名罪由抓捕，并被送某教育集中营以接受“政治再教育”；<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，获悉其已在同年早些时候被新疆塔城地区法院秘密重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">19</span>年，</b>罪名不详，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2037</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日。目前被羁押地点或服刑监狱缺详。判刑之前其在被判刑前曾被迫认罪，家属遭软禁，探视权被剥夺，沙湾县纪委（中共纪律检查委员会）竟称如要让其释放，家属须交保释金<span lang="EN-US">40</span>万元人民币。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">哈里斯别克·巴班（哈）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1987</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年出生，新疆维吾尔自治区昌吉回族自治州呼图壁县人，哈萨克族，新疆乌鲁木齐市居民，哈萨克民歌手，中国在押良心犯。身为一哈萨克族歌手，因喜欢传唱民族歌曲而深受亲友及当地民众的好评；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年，因曾到昌吉州吉木萨尔县泉子街镇吾塘沟村<span lang="EN-US">1</span>号参加表演，在表演会上演唱了“得罪中共当局”的歌曲，随遭到中共新疆当局的强力打压；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，被乌鲁木齐市警方以涉嫌“宣扬非法宗教等罪”抓捕，并被指控唱了政府认为“不该唱的歌曲”；据悉，自被捕后一直失联，家属不知其具体案情，只知至今尚未判刑，但又不被释放。目前被羁押于呼图壁县监狱。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">哈木拉提<span lang="EN-US">.</span>吾甫尔</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：男，维吾尔族，<span lang="EN-US">1960</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月出生，研究生医学博士，“国家长江学者创新团队发展计划”发起者，曾任“新疆医科大学校长”。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年曾入选中国科学院院士曾选初步候选人名单，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月任新疆食药监局局长。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，最后一次在媒体上露面。现被证实，已被乌鲁木齐警方以“传播极端民族主义思想”罪由被抓，至今下落不明。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">哈纳提别克•萨布尔别克（哈萨克）、哈伊拉提别克•木合塔尔汗（哈萨克）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">二人与</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">纳杂尔﹒叶尔江、阿尔恒﹒巴杂尔别克、乌木别提﹒卡斯木、沙部旦﹒沙伊合、耶尔肯别克﹒达列力、肯杰别克﹒达列力、玛乌提﹒么斯尔汗都是新疆伊利市哈萨克自治州阿尔泰市巴里巴盖乡人，哈萨克族，穆斯林。其中，纳杂尔﹒叶尔江<span lang="EN-US">26</span>岁，哈纳提别克﹒萨布尔别克<span lang="EN-US">26</span>岁，阿尔恒﹒巴杂尔别克<span lang="EN-US">27</span>岁，乌木别提﹒卡斯木<span lang="EN-US">31</span>岁，哈伊拉提别克﹒木合塔尔汗<span lang="EN-US">37</span>岁，沙部旦﹒沙伊合约<span lang="EN-US">30</span>岁，耶尔肯别克﹒达列力<span lang="EN-US">30</span>岁，肯杰别克﹒达列力<span lang="EN-US">27</span>岁，玛乌提﹒么斯尔汗约<span lang="EN-US">30</span>岁。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span
