lang="EN-US">-8</span>月，因他们分别在私下里进行了穆斯林传统常规祷告仪式，而被中共新疆伊犁市哈萨克自治州阿尔泰当局知晓后拘捕，遂很快被阿尔泰市地方法院以“非法从事宗教活动”和“从事宗教极端活动”为由分别判处<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">-6</span>年不等刑期。目前各人具体判刑不详，刑至日期不详，服刑监狱不详，服刑状况及健康程度等不详。</span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">海莱提•尼亚孜（维吾尔）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1960</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年出生，新疆维吾尔自治区塔城市人，原《新疆法制报》总编室主任、《法治纵横》杂志社副社长、《新疆经济报》前记者，原“维吾尔在线”网站的编辑和管理员以及维吾尔在线论坛版主，维吾尔著名媒体人，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年，乌鲁木齐<span lang="EN-US">7</span>•<span lang="EN-US">5</span>事件后因多次接受包括香港《亚洲周刊》在内的采访，分析新疆骚乱的深层次原因，批评时任自治区书记王乐泉治理政策不当，并透露自己曾经在<span lang="EN-US">7.5 </span>前一天向新疆领导部门提出过预警却未被采纳等，遂于<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日被警方从乌鲁木齐家中抓走，关押在乌鲁木齐天山看守所；<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日其家人收到当局的拘捕通知书，随后被乌鲁木齐法院以“危害国家安全罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">15</span>年。现在新疆昌吉监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">海米提·阿不都热合曼（维）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1954</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月出生，新疆维吾尔自治区伊犁哈萨克自治州伊宁市人，维吾尔族名<span lang="EN-US">Haimiti Abudureheman</span>，原伊犁州邮电局退休干部，中国在押良心犯。被捕前从未参与过政治维权或请愿活动，为人忠厚老实，深得其子女的爱戴及信任；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年，曾与妻子沙阿呆提<span lang="EN-US">.</span>巴吴顿二人到土耳其旅行，并与已在瑞典流亡且参与政治维权和申请了政治庇护的儿子托格鲁克·海米提见过面，返回新疆时，因当时新疆并未出现“政治再教育营”之说，故其行踪随被当局知晓，但并未被伊宁市警方问讯或传唤训诫，就此二人一直相安无事；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2017</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年，随着中共当局在新疆出现大规模清理少数民族宗教文化行动以来，新疆各地越来越多的推出了“政治思想再教育营”（又称“政治再教育中心”）计划，其曾经出国探亲之举（即曾与成为政治难民的儿子见面），使其即刻变成当局仇视和需要严打报复的对象；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，其夫妇二人双双被伊犁哈萨克自治州伊宁市警方带走，并送某“政治再教育中心”羁押，自此失联；<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，知其被伊宁市警方以“与在海外申请政治庇护的儿子会面”为罪由逮捕，近期被新疆伊犁州伊宁市法院重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">18</span>年，罪名不详，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2035</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日；</b>据悉，其在看守所内身体健康状况极差；其在乌鲁木齐市一家银行工作的女儿遭牵连，亦于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日被强制送进“政治再教育中心”接受洗脑式教育，至今下落不明。目前服刑监狱不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">郝福奎：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辽宁大连法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，大连公安局国保支队同大连开发区公安分局属下五彩城派出所、湾里派出所、黄海路派出所、海青派出所、董家沟派出所等出动数十个警察，以拦路抓捕、抢劫、入室抢劫的方式在多个地点同时实施多起抓捕法轮功学员案。十名当时被抓捕的法轮功学员被非法批捕：周海燕、胡志琴（女，五十八岁）、来桂芳（女，四十二岁）、时宁瑶（女，三十八岁）、方芳（女，五十四岁）、林景萍（女，四十六岁）、贾秀春（女，四十一岁）、曹娥（女，五十五岁）、武丽艳（女，五十二岁）和刘淑芬（女，七十八岁）。八十一岁的郝福奎<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日被取保候审。后<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月八名法轮功学员被大连开发区法院判刑：周海燕<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，胡志琴<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年半，来桂芳<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，时宁瑶<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，林景萍<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，方芳<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半，郝福奎<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，贾秀春<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。郝福奎刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">郝劲松：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山西“知名法律人士”。郝劲松生于<span lang="EN-US">1972</span>年，山西忻州人。著名人权律师。郝劲松律师自<span lang="EN-US">2004</span>年开始先后<span lang="EN-US">7</span>次将国家税务总局、北京地铁运营公司、北京铁路局告上法庭，原他因对“打破行业‘霸王条款’起到了一定作用”而入选“<span lang="EN-US">2004</span>年构建经济和谐十大受尊崇人物”。郝劲松被先后提名为<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>中国法制新闻人物，<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年度十大法制人物，并以“维权战士”的身份写入《<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>中国法治蓝皮书》。因介入推动铁道部春运不涨价案件入选《<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>中国法治蓝皮书》，并当选<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>中国十大消费维权人物，<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年因介入陕西华南虎案件和杨佳案被《南方人物周刊》评选为“中国魅力人物——公义之魅”。<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年，介入上海“钓鱼执法事件”。后成立山西定襄县劲松法务咨询中心。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年，郝劲松向定襄县环保局实名举报当地的诚泰纺织印染公司涉嫌污染空气和水源。郝劲松于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日、<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日就连续两天遭到户籍地山西省定襄县晋昌镇派出所以“寻衅滋事”为由传唤后，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日再遭该派出所传唤。随后被行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，行政拘留期满被转刑事拘留，控罪为涉嫌寻衅滋事。后遭正式逮捕。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">郝明媚：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">又名郝英吾，黑龙江省大庆法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年五十三岁，从事英语教师职业，原住黑龙江省北安市。于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日下午，遭到大庆市公安局警察抓捕，后被以“利用邪教扰乱公共秩序”的罪起诉到大庆市让胡路区检察院，被批捕。于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日判郝明媚<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年有期徒刑，并敲诈勒索两万元。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">韩爱珍：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辽宁省朝阳市龙城区下河首村法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年五十六岁的韩爱珍，是位朴实忠厚的农村妇女。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日晚，韩爱珍与刘欣在粘贴大法真相时，被蹲坑的新华分局警察抓捕，并遭抄家，被关押在朝阳市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，韩爱珍被朝阳市龙城法院判处<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年有期徒刑，刘欣判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>缓<span lang="EN-US">5</span>释放回家。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">韩建海：男，</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2019</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">62</span>岁，辽宁省大连市沙河口区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日晚九点左右，张仁光、王尚杰、韩建海、李静波<span lang="EN-US">,4</span>人因发真相资料，分别被国保和民权派出所绑架。在张仁光家抄走大量耗材。后全送姚家看守所。大连市沙河口区法院<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日庭审法轮功学员张仁光、王尚杰、韩建海、李静波，并判韩建海<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年、勒索罚款<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">韩良：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">重庆公民，于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日到<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，两天在巴南区民主广场宣传法治，捍卫人权，<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日在渝中区奥体广场宣传法治，进行“捍卫人权”的演讲，于<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日失去联系。本网几经周折最近获知韩良已被重庆当局刑事拘留，目前羁押在渝中区看守所。重庆公民韩良系<span lang="EN-US">49</span>年生人，现已年近七旬。他自称是国军军官后代，长期游走街头讲抗战史，讲历史真相，宣传法治人权。因与官方的版本有出入而受到重庆公安打压。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年，韩良曾因上街纪念“抗战胜利<span lang="EN-US">68</span>周年”被公安打伤。去年重庆选举基层人大代表期间，韩良作为独立参选人竞选人大代表，遭到当局刁难，后来韩良也因此被拘留。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日“世界人权日”前夕，韩良被当地公安局以“扰乱公共场所秩序”处以行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">韩猛<span lang="EN-US">: </span></span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河南政府信息公开申请人、知名民间维权举报打假人王清同案。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，被南阳市卧龙区警方以涉嫌“敲诈勒索罪”刑拘。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，本案被南阳市卧龙区检察院移交至南阳市卧龙区法院进行起诉；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，其王清、陈强、王聚才及韩猛<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人被以涉“敲诈勒索案”在南阳市卧龙区法院开庭受审，后韩猛被该法院一审以“敲诈勒索罪”枉法重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，韩猛刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">韩雪松：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辽宁省营口市鲅鱼圈区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日中午<span lang="EN-US">11</span>点，法轮功学员金翠香开着松花江小面包车，载着韩雪松（<span lang="EN-US">49</span>岁）、韩美玲（<span lang="EN-US">62</span>岁）、柳爱敏（<span lang="EN-US">56</span>岁）、徐笑岩行进在大连瓦房店李官镇的街道上，突然一辆警车拦截，随即围过来六七个警察，在车上搜出两小摞《九评》书。几名法轮功学员被抓捕到李官镇派出所。后刑拘逮捕起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日瓦房店法院判<span lang="EN-US">5</span>位法轮功学员：金翠香<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年并罚款<span lang="EN-US">8000</span>元；韩雪松<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月并罚款<span lang="EN-US">8000</span>元；韩美玲<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年并罚款<span lang="EN-US">5000</span>元；柳爱敏<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年并罚款<span lang="EN-US">3000</span>元；徐笑岩、柳爱敏已获释。韩雪松刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">杭霞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">合肥法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日杭霞被抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月开庭未判。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月，合肥瑶海区法院近期到看守所向杭霞单独宣判：判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。不准上诉。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">何观娇：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2020</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日晚，何观娇和妹妹何水姑到福州动车北站，买了<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>号（大年二十九）早上<span lang="EN-US">7</span>点<span lang="EN-US">10</span>分由福州北站来往北京西的动车。等待到第二天（<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>号）早上离动车发车的前半个小时，何氏姐妹俩在福州火车站南广场，被一帮人共计六个人强行绑架到一辆白色私家车上。今年已经<span lang="EN-US">54</span>岁的何观娇，是上世纪七十年代因中越关系恶化而跟父母归国的侨民。<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年到<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年，何观娇分别在深圳市宝安区公明镇摩打制造厂和深圳市飞狮电子工业有限公司工作，因为长期接触有毒胶水，导致呼吸困难，多次昏倒，差一点死掉。何观娇多次要求用人单位调换工种被拒绝，加上得不到积极治疗，终失去劳动能力，被用人单位赶出厂门，到劳动仲裁部门要求进行工伤鉴定，被拒绝，遂开始了上访之路。由于何观娇在福州市晋安区新店镇横厝<span lang="EN-US">24</span>号<span lang="EN-US">20</span>座<span lang="EN-US">302</span>（福州北郊华侨塑料二厂）的房屋又遭强拆，且没有得到政府的任何安置，一直借住在姐姐妹妹家中。为了维护自己的合法权益，何观娇趁春节乘车方便，遂于大年二十九购买动车票，准备再次进京信访，却遭绑架失踪。后获知其被关在福州神康精神病院。在何水姑跟福州神康精神病院医生通电话过程中，被告知是公安将其强制送到精神病院的。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">何华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">贵阳市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">55</span>岁的何华女士，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日向路人发送<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年新年挂历，被巡逻特警抓捕，先被关押在贵阳市云岩区拘留所，后转到贵阳市云岩区看守所。先判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，后检察院抗诉，又于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日贵阳市中级法院又改判何华<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">何菊英：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1964</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日出生，湖南省宁远县人，湖南省宁远县中和镇上街村村民，维权访民，<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年，曾因其上初中的儿子被学校的几位恶少殴打致残，遭地方法院枉法判决，遂走上了漫长艰辛的维权之路；之后又因其上访的行为触碰了地方当局的利益神经，故而遭到地方当局的严酷打压，并因此屡遭非法关押；<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年和<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年，曾两次因上访维权遭遇政府枉法构陷，被先后处以劳动教养共计<span lang="EN-US">30</span>个月，并被多次关押于精神病院和黑监狱；<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年，曾因被关在教养所内，其家中老人无人照顾且遭到当局的恶意骚扰和恐吓，致使两位老人在惊吓过度和贫病交加中相继去世。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，当其再次到北京上访时，被地方当局从北京截访并强行遣回原籍，随后被警方以“非法上访”为罪由处以行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日；<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，又被以涉嫌“敲诈勒索政府罪”刑事拘留；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，被湖南省宁远县检察院以同罪名正式批捕。目前被羁押于湖南省宁远县看守所，未审待判。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">何林夏：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">广西师范大学出版社集团前董事长，此出版社是大陆最先锋和最前卫的出版社，其打造的“理想国”、“魔法象”、“新民说”品牌也在读者和知识分子群体中享有很高的知名度。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，广西检察院官方微信公众平台发布消息：日前，广西壮族自治区人民检察院依法以涉嫌受贿罪对广西师范大学出版社集团原董事长何林夏（正处级）决定逮捕，案件侦查工作正在进行中。据知情人士透露<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月中旬何林夏就被逮捕了，与出版社年初计划出版已故历史学家高华的遗作和独立导演张赞波的作品《大路》被叫停有关，作为董事长的何林夏疑被秋后算帐。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2019</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，本网获悉：<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，广西灌阳县人民法院以所谓贪污罪判处何林夏有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10 </span>年，这和其出版一些当局认为比较危险的书有关。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">何雪荣：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">甘肃省庆城县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，甘肃省庆阳市庆城县法轮功学员何雪荣与其丈夫到西峰区彭原乡粘贴法轮功不干胶时，遭当地一村支书恶告，被彭原乡派出所警察绑架，后转到庆城县公安局，后其丈夫已回家，何雪荣已被拘禁于庆城县看守所，已被宣布正式逮捕。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">何正琼：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">四川省凉山州西昌市法轮功学员何正琼（<span lang="EN-US">54</span>岁）于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日下午<span lang="EN-US">7</span>点左右，在宁远桥附近讲法轮大法，被一群不明真相的小学生围住，并打<span lang="EN-US">110</span>报警。后来了一辆警车，下来两个警察。何正琼抱住电线杆不配合上车，被警察用小瓶状物喷眼睛（可能类似胡椒水），强行抬上车。后被西昌市国安绑架到西昌市拓荒戒毒所非法关押。因修炼法轮功，此前何正琼被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年初才刑满出狱。她的亲家母胡云怀<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年在拓荒看守所被迫害致死，姑姑何先珍被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，在四川省简阳养马河女子监狱被迫害成植物人，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日凌晨五点过在四川省金堂警察医院（监狱医院）含冤离世。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">何宗旺：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">福建省福清市的公民，长期致力于为弱势群体发声。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年在北京经营药材生意的他因为转发金水桥事件的帖子被刑拘<span lang="EN-US">37</span>天。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年开始参与线下围观，<span lang="EN-US">4.29</span>苏州拜祭林昭，到郑州旁听贾灵敏案庭审。两度赴庆安围观徐纯合案，期间被拘留十天。“<span lang="EN-US">709</span>”系列案的潍坊案中被捕。潍坊看守所内遭受连续六天的疲劳审讯，关押近三个月后脊椎囊肿爆裂，导致下肢瘫痪且大小便失禁。潍坊看守所将其送院后，通知其家人取保接回福建老家治疗，留下后遗症。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，何宗旺在福州市第一看守所门口迎接刑满获释的严兴声时被抓捕，关押在福州市第二看守所。当局先抓捕再寻找罗织罪证，他们以何宗旺在<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月闽清水灾过后进入灾区了解灾区情况为由，以“编造、故意传播虚假信息罪”执行逮捕，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月将其转往闽清看守所关押。<span lang="EN-US">019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，何宗旺被闽清法院以“编造、故意传播虚假信息罪、寻衅滋事罪”两个罪名分别判处<span lang="EN-US">2.5</span>年和<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，合并执行<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年有期徒刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"> <o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">贺英：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">她与贾灵娟都是山西省汾西县人，法轮功学员。因信仰和宣传法轮功，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日上午，其二人在汾西县永安镇店头村宣传法轮功时，被人用手机照相上网恶告，而被永安镇派出所警察抓捕、抄家。两人现被关押在汾西县看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黑伊特：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黑伊特于<span lang="EN-US">1964</span>年在新疆喀什市出生，是著名的维吾尔族诗人及音乐家，擅长弹奏都塔尔琴，他的歌曲描绘维吾尔族历史文化，在土耳其也有知名度；他在<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年创作《父亲》一曲，歌词提及「战争烈士」，后被抓捕。据悉其被中国当局认为是极端分子，在未经起诉下判囚<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">洪桂连：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">安徽省计生牺牲品和政府不作为乱作为受害人。洪桂连因计划生育国策两次被黄山市屯溪区强制堕胎，此后唯一的儿子又因政府疏于安全生产管理，导致采砂船滥采滥挖河砂，导致家乡河道出现危险溺水而亡，为此洪上访维权，被迫接受政府所谓救助金，却被翻手为云覆手为雨的政府定为敲诈勒索罪。洪桂连出狱后申诉、控告无门，就赴京上访，从北京返家后的第二天就被警方以所谓网上逃犯名义抓捕，然后移交给安徽省黄山市警方，现在羁押于黄山市看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">洪柳：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">重庆法轮功学员。母亲邓吉琼家住重庆市渝北区，林忠英家住重庆市巴南区。由于中共在法轮功学员的身份证上做标注，法轮功学员的正常出行时时受监控、骚扰。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日一早，邓吉琼与未修炼法轮功的丈夫洪代鹏，乘高铁到成都。验票时，邓吉琼的身份证提示其法轮功学员的身份，邓吉琼和丈夫遭火车站人员拦截抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，邓吉琼亲家母林忠英也被抓捕，次日<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，邓吉琼的儿子、林忠英的女婿洪柳被抓捕。他们被关押一年多后，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，邓吉琼被重庆市江北区法院判处<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年有期徒刑，洪柳被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，林忠英被判<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，三人同时被勒索罚金。洪柳刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">洪永忠</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：广东省海丰县人，广东省海丰县乌坎村民维权代表。<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月曾因所在广东省海丰县乌坎村村民不满当局私自非法变卖村民土地，获利<span lang="EN-US">9</span>亿元且被村干部分摊，从而引发举世关注的乌坎事件，又因乌坎村民多次举行大规模维权游行示威，推行村民民主选举制度，并与警方数次爆发大型反抗冲突，遂遭广东当局的疯狂报复，<span lang="EN-US">70</span>余人被抓、被通缉，其亦被广东当局定为“乌坎魏永汉、洪永忠等<span lang="EN-US">9</span>人聚众扰乱社会秩序，非法集会、游行、示威，聚众扰乱交通秩序，妨害公务，故意传播虚假信息案”首要分子。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日被网上通缉，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月下旬被陆丰县警方以涉嫌多种聚众扰乱社会秩序罪由拘捕，后转正式逮捕。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日其案件在广东省海丰县法院开庭受审，至<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日被广东省海丰县法院一审以“非法集会、游行、示威罪”、“聚众扰乱社会秩序罪”、“妨害公务罪”等多项罪名，判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，控其“聚众扰乱社会秩序，情节严重，致使生产、营业无法进行，造成严重损失”。目前被羁押于海丰县公安局看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">候敏玲</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">汶川地震甘肃的灾民。候敏玲也是在<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年敏感时期被抓回当地，至今没有准确消息。候敏玲在长期维权过程中，成为了访民社区的爱心人士，给新访民提供各种各样的方便与帮助。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">侯巧珍：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河北邯郸市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年已七十七岁，是邯郸市一位退休教师。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日下午，侯巧珍与张培英在邯郸市复兴区彭家寨附近讲述法轮功被迫害真相时，被告发，遭复兴区公安分局彭家寨派出所抓捕，被关押在邯郸市第三看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，邯郸市磁县法院在邯郸第三看守所里暗箱操作，对侯巧珍和张培英开庭，后判侯巧珍<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年有期徒刑，张培英<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>个月。侯巧珍刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 44.25pt;"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">胡光珍：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1969</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日出生，湖北枣阳人，访民领袖。丧偶多年，丈夫和孩子都曾是军人，家住湖北省枣阳市西园三组。因与开发商的拆迁协议纠纷上访，长期以来，胡光珍维权和帮助身边的人维权。曾被拘留<span lang="EN-US">9</span>次，遭不明身份人士非法拘禁<span lang="EN-US">30</span>天。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，因在北京上访被地方截访人员遣返原籍，并拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天。同年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，又被以涉嫌<span lang="EN-US">“</span>敲诈勒索罪<span lang="EN-US">”</span>刑拘，关押在枣阳第一看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日被转正式逮捕。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日胡光珍案在没有通知近亲家属的情况下开庭，至<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，最终被枣阳市法院以其多次去北京上访告状罪由，以<span lang="EN-US">“</span>敲诈勒索罪<span lang="EN-US">”</span>判处<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月刑期。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">胡功</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：<span lang="EN-US">1962</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日出生，内蒙古自治区呼和浩特市玉泉区人，原呼和浩特市回民区义和巷“芬芳理发店”理发师，曾被当地报纸誉为“<span lang="EN-US">25</span>年义务理发的好市民”，基督徒，呼和浩特市基督教“呼喊派”召会负责人，中国在押良心犯。曾因信仰有争议的基督教地方召会“呼喊派”，拥有“呼喊派”书籍，并与他人积极散发<span lang="EN-US">800</span>百余份福音宣传资料，触动了中共当局加强意识形态、信仰自由控制的敏感神经，随于<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日被呼和浩特市玉泉区警方从居住地带走，<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日被以涉嫌“组织、利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”刑事拘留，被关押于内蒙古自治区呼和浩特市第三看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，又被以同罪名正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，其涉嫌“邪教案”被内蒙古自治区呼和浩特市玉泉区检察院提起公诉，被控以“小排聚会、主日聚会、婚礼聚会、境外特会进行聚集，通过电子邮件接收境外的邪教资料，与境外的邪教人员进行非法联系”；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，最终被呼和浩特市玉泉区法院以“组织和利用邪教破坏国家法律实施”罪重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年；其不服上诉，<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日经呼和浩特市中级法院二审宣判，依然维持原判。目前具体服刑监狱不详。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">胡石根</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：<span lang="EN-US">1954</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日出生，江西省南昌市人，基督徒，北京基督教家庭教会圣爱团契、中原教会、雅和博教会长老，独立中文笔会关注会员，中国著名民主异议人士。<span lang="EN-US">1991</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月曾与王国齐秘密成立中国自由民主党，并参与康玉春等人成立的“中华进步同盟”；<span lang="EN-US">1991</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月曾与刘京生、高玉祥等人共同成立“中国自由工会筹备委员会”；<span lang="EN-US">1992</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月—<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月曾计划到北京、上海、武汉等地散发传单，并利用航模直升机在天安门广场空投传单，以抗议中共六四屠杀事件和纪念六四死难者，<span lang="EN-US">1992</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日被北京警方刑拘，同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日被以涉“组织、领导反革命集团罪”和“反革命宣传煽动罪”正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">1994</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日被北京市中级法院以两罪名重判<span lang="EN-US">20</span>年，并在北京市第二监狱服刑，服刑期间身心因遭受巨大迫害曾一度病危，至<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，被提前减刑获释。出狱后，因继续追求民主自由，关注、参与全国性劳工维权事件及公民活动，广结正义维权律师，又因笃信基督教而成为北京基督教家庭教会圣爱团契的传道人，遂一直遭当局传唤、软禁及强迫失踪等严打迫害；<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年曾因支持“中国茉莉花革命”而被警方秘押，并遭警方戴黑头套、殴打和威胁等；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日曾因参加“六四纪念研讨会”而被当局以涉“寻衅滋事罪”传唤，且被刑拘一个月；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日再次被北京警方传唤，自此失联，其家被抄，后得知其已于<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日被当局以涉“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”和“寻衅滋事罪”指定居所监视居住；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日被天津市警方正式逮捕，并关押在天津市第一看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日被天津市第二中级法院以“颠覆国家政权罪”重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，剥权<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。目前在天津市长泰监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">胡湘银：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">江西宜春公民、残疾人胡湘银因积极参加维权行动<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日被刑事拘留的，已于<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日被以诈骗罪批捕。胡湘银因为<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年介绍两位公民代理帮人打宅基地官司，当时因没达到对方要求（要四块地当地只给一块）。当事人因此恼怒告他们诈骗，后不了了之。后来在今年八月份胡因组织当地维权人士到上海声援一个被判刑的维权人士，结果被选择性“执法”抓捕。目前他家人生活困难也缺律师，需要援助。胡湘银是残疾人<span lang="EN-US">(</span>童年时双手被高压电击伤造成<span lang="EN-US">)</span>，靠开摩的维持一家五口的生计<span lang="EN-US">:</span>瞻养<span lang="EN-US">80</span>多岁的老母亲，抚养两个小孩<span lang="EN-US">(</span>最小的才满<span lang="EN-US">4</span>岁<span lang="EN-US">)</span>，尽管如此，他还是热心于公民维权，一有时间就积极参与维权行动。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">胡勇：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">湖北钟祥市人，基督教华南教会（<span lang="EN-US">SCC</span>）创建人及钟祥交通会骨干成员。曾因其与龚圣亮、徐福明等人共同组建基督教华南家庭教会，是湖北省荆门市钟祥市教会的骨干成员，并积极力促该教会在活动范围和信徒人数等方面迅速发展，随引起中共当局的极度恐慌和强烈不满，在把华南教会定性为“邪教组织”的同时，亦对其及其多名教会骨干成员施以严酷的打击；<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，因与徐福明等人一起被控涉嫌“参与<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月在湖北省钟祥市对受害人谢东报复伤害案”，而被荆门市钟祥市警方以“利用邪教破坏法律实施罪”刑拘，<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日被正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日被湖北省荆门市中级法院一审以同罪名判处死刑；<span lang="EN-US">2002</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日又经湖北省荆门市中级法院二审，以“故意伤害罪”改判为无期徒刑，剥夺政治权利终身。目前在湖北省某监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">胡友刚：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吉林省洮南市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，法轮功学员胡友刚、田超夫妇在洮南市的家被抄家，当天胡友刚被送入白城市看守所关押，田超被送入镇赉县看守所非法关押。胡友刚被关押一年多，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>也底才得知被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，已于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月被送至吉林省公主岭市监狱。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">胡占亭：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1949</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年出生，辽宁阜新市人，法轮功信仰者，良心犯。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，因粘贴有关法轮功宣传信息，被辽宁省阜新市海州区法院以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”枉法判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，曾因粘贴有关法轮功的真实信息，被阜新市海州区警方秘密跟踪抓捕，家被查抄，后被海州区检察院以涉嫌“邪教罪”批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日其涉邪教案在阜新市海州区法院开庭受理，律师虽然为其做了辩护，但法庭却剥夺了胡占亭本人的辩护权，最终他被阜新市海州区法院以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”重判刑期<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。其不服上诉，但阜新市中级法院却故意绕开律师，草草暗中非法宣判，维持原判<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日其被送到锦州监狱服刑，后于同年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日前又被秘密转监到沈阳市第一监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">胡志琴：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辽宁大连法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，大连公安局国保支队同大连开发区公安分局属下五彩城派出所、湾里派出所、黄海路派出所、海青派出所、董家沟派出所等出动数十个警察，以拦路抓捕、抢劫、入室抢劫的方式在多个地点同时实施多起抓捕法轮功学员案。十名当时被抓捕的法轮功学员被非法批捕：周海燕、胡志琴（女，五十八岁）、来桂芳（女，四十二岁）、时宁瑶（女，三十八岁）、方芳（女，五十四岁）、林景萍（女，四十六岁）、贾秀春（女，四十一岁）、曹娥（女，五十五岁）、武丽艳（女，五十二岁）和刘淑芬（女，七十八岁）。八十一岁的郝福奎<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日被取保候审。后<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月八名法轮功学员被大连开发区法院判刑：周海燕<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，胡志琴<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年半，来桂芳<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，时宁瑶<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，林景萍<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，方芳<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半，郝福奎<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，贾秀春<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。胡志琴刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黄安阳：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">他与</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">邓洪成、肖兵、王军、沈力、李南海（火焱）、丁岩、王威、王建华、李江鹏等广东深圳<span lang="EN-US">10</span>公民遭抓捕。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">以上<span lang="EN-US">10</span>人在<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日后连续遭拘捕或强迫失踪。后警方向追寻下落的邓洪成、王军家属证实其已被羁押，被指涉颠覆。后被告知指定居所监视居住。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黄根吉：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东省青岛市即墨区田横镇法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，即墨公安局以将要召开青岛峰会“维稳”为借口，没出示任何证件，闯入黄根吉家抄家。后将黄根吉抓捕到即墨普东看守所关押。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月，山东省青岛市即墨区法院对黄根吉判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黄光玉</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：女，<span lang="EN-US">52</span>岁，湖南省吉首市镇溪办事处吉新社区吉新村豹子孔组村民，维权访民。早年曾因政府规划不当，导致邻居建房与她发生纠纷，后一直希望政府解决问题未果，随其逐级上访维权。但又因她频繁上访，所以屡遭吉首市政府的严打，曾被枉法劳教<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年。获释后，她继续上访维权。因吉首市政府为顾及政绩和自身利益，让其息诉罢访，于是很快双方达成经济补偿协议，并进行了公证处公证，然而直到<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月吉首市政府也没对此协议予以履行，迫使其继续进京投诉。却不料竟又被北京警方以 “扰乱公共场所秩序”为由给予行政处罚。同年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日当其在北京天安门寻找遭行政处罚时遗失的视频资料时，被赶来的截访人员劫持，并在遣送回去后再次被吉首市警方行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日行拘届满日，没被释放被吉首市警方又以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日其案被吉首市检察院更换罪名，以涉“敲诈勒索罪”起诉至吉首市法院，至<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日日被吉首市法院以“敲诈勒索罪”一审判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，经湖南省湘西土家族苗族自治州中级法院二审裁决，依然维持原判。目前被羁押于湘西自治州看守所，不久将送往湖南长沙女子监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黄红萍<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">江苏启东市<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年五十一岁的法轮功学员，南京河海大学化学系八九届毕业生，原在启东盖天力制药厂工作，因坚持修炼法轮功，被单位开除，住南通市启东市寅阳镇临海桥村。黄红萍多次遭“<span lang="EN-US">610</span>”（专门迫害法轮功的非法组织）与公安警察残酷迫害。黄红萍女士曾被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年后，出狱才几个月又被绑架，又被判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年。近四年的迫害，致使她精神上、身体上遭受严重摧残，监狱医院诊断黄红萍得了宫颈癌。在南通监狱生命垂危。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，家属要求放黄红萍回家治疗，监狱负责人说，要写所谓“三书”才可以放人。所谓的“三书”就是悔过书、决心书、保证书。黄红萍表示坚修大法，决不写三书，目前在南通某医院。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黄金桔：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">她与赵文静、吕月霞、郭春该及张迪<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">为涉</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河南省商丘巿宁陵县双庙村教会教案成员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日该教会一座兴建中的教堂，遭到数百名政府人员强拆，双方发生争执，教会物品被毁坏，信徒被打伤，数十人包括该<span lang="EN-US">5</span>名负责人被公安带走，后这<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人被拘留。他们被指涉嫌“寻衅滋事”及“非法拘禁”罪，<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日被县检察院正式逮捕。其中张迪是临近一教会的传道人，为协助该教会建教堂，而遭牵连得。目前，所有被捕者被羁押在宁陵县看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，该教会成立<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，信徒百多人，当局曾要求加入三自教会不遂。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 360.75pt;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><span style="mso-tab-count: 1;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黄兰凤：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">佳士事件”被捕人士，佳士被捕工人余浚聪妻子<b>。</b>被捕是由于一直坚持为丈夫李展发声，以及继续声援佳士工人维权遭到报复抓捕。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黄连：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">广东省湛江市雷州市纪家镇上郎村人，原纪家镇制板厂工人，法轮功学员。因控告前中共党魁江泽民发动迫害法轮功，<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日被广东省湛江市雷州市国保队长等<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人绑架，家被查抄，搜走电脑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>台、打印机<span lang="EN-US">4</span>部、录音机<span lang="EN-US">2</span>部及个人所有法轮功书籍资料等私人物品。被关押在雷州市看守所期间，因黄连绝食抗议，曾遭到强行鼻饲迫害，身体非常虚弱。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月，黄连的家人收到判决书，得知黄连已被湛江市雷州市法院以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。其不服提起上诉，二审维持原判。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黄俊娟：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">天津法轮功学员。家住武清区上马台镇王老庄村。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，黄俊娟在善良的向百姓传法时被抓捕，关押在武清看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，被武清法院非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，并罚金勒索一万元。黄俊娟不服，已上诉。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><br /></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黄琦：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">六四天网人权事务中心创始人、负责人。黄琦<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日晚于家中被带走，其义工蒲飞也失联。<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日晚<span lang="EN-US">9</span>时许被来自棉阳、内江和成都南站派出所的警察<span lang="EN-US">15</span>人闯入家中带走。黄琦<span lang="EN-US">1963</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日生，中国四川人，黄琦毕业于四川大学无线电子系，<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>年成立了“天网寻人事务所”，<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年设立“六四天网”网站。由于网站同时还登载各种批评时政的文章，引发中国当局的关注。<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日即六四事件十一周年纪念日的前一天，黄琦被警察捕。在被捕近三年后，<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，成都市中级人民法院以煽动颠覆国家政权罪，判处黄琦有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，黄琦刑满获释。<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，黄琦改组六四天网为中国天网人权事务中心。<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年中国汶川大地震后，黄琦积极参与救灾活动，同时为地震中死亡学生的家长提供帮助，而且在网上撰文揭露“豆腐渣”工程。<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日晚，黄琦和天网人权事务中心两名工作人员吃饭时被几名身份不明的人强行塞进一辆汽车带走。后被控「非法持有国家机密」受到刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，黄琦以非法持有国家机密罪名被正式起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日成都市武侯区法院对黄琦案进行了宣判，法院以“非法持有国家机密档罪”，判处黄琦有期徒刑三年。<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日黄琦刑满出狱，现定居于成都。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日中共十八大六中全会前夜间与外界失联。后被证实遭随州国保强制传唤。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日上午，著名人权捍卫者、六四天网负责人黄琦被四川省绵阳市法院以“故意泄露国家秘密罪”及“为境外非法提供国家秘密罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，没收个人财产<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元。其中“故意泄露国家秘密罪”<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，“为境外非法提供国家秘密罪”<span lang="EN-US">11</span>年，数罪并罚执行<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年有期徒刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黄信：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">安徽省界首市拆迁访民。黄信与界首市其他访民于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月初赴京上访，返回界首市家中于<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日被警察抓走，并被警方抄走家中的信访资料。当晚<span lang="EN-US">19</span>时黄信被界首市公安局决定以“涉嫌敲诈勒索罪”刑拘，送界首市看守所羁押。据悉黄信就房屋拆迁之事此前起诉界首市东城街道办事处的行政案件一审胜诉。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 351.75pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黄秀兰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">曾用名黄秀梅，<span lang="EN-US">1971</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日出生，住商丘市睢阳区，个体业主。作为法轮功修炼者。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，黄秀兰女士在商丘市睢阳区香君路与凯旋路交叉口向一个路人发了一本<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年的吉祥娃娃新年台历。此人叫任文珠，是睢阳区街道办事处工作人员。她诬告黄女士，先是打电话给社区主任，后叫来了商丘市新城公安分局警察和商丘睢阳国保大队警察。她一直跟踪黄女士陆陆续续叫了好多人，最后在几里地之外的县城里一个洗衣机维修店绑架了正在修洗衣机的黄女士并非法抄了她的家。连她的姐夫和孩子都没有放过，一并绑架到看守所迫害。公安警察在敲诈勒索了家人几万元钱后才放两个人回家，在此案中却被成为“证人”。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日下午<span lang="EN-US">2</span>，河南商丘睢阳区法院对法轮功学员黄秀兰的进行了庭审。来自云南的维权律师出庭为黄秀兰女士做无罪辩护，首先对此次庭审检察院、法院故意刁难、为难律师拒不接受律师正规的合法手续，差点非法剥夺当事人和律师的辩护权深表遗憾。在法庭辩论过程中，律师逐条驳斥了公诉人的指控。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黄雅珍</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：辽宁省本溪市女法轮功学员燕文芹、黄雅珍、于金凤被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，三人已提出上诉。燕文芹、黄雅珍、于金凤均已六十多岁，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，只因向世人赠送几本台历，被本溪县碱厂派出所绑架并非法拘留，期限未到，竟然直接转为刑拘。在本溪市看守所关押期间，被强迫每天长时间做奴工，完不成任务就罚站。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，本溪县法院对三人非法开庭。律师指出：公安人员将当事人行政拘留直接转为刑事拘留，是违法行为，是绑架，应撤销他们的违法行为。因公安机关捏造罪名、违法办案，庭审无法继续，草草收场。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，本溪县法院对被非法关押近一年的三位老人再次开庭，家属聘请了三位知名律师作无罪辩护。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黄云敏：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黄云敏是新疆生产建设兵团农三师图木舒克市的退休法官，因帮助农三师农场职工维权，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日被以“煽动民族仇恨、民族歧视罪”拘捕。黄云敏案曾于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日在新疆生产建设兵团喀什农垦法院开庭。后获知黄云敏被转送“法律援助中心”接受所谓的思想教育。并未有判刑信息。后获知，黄云敏因替百姓维权获刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年。（<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日黄云敏因会见时告知其妻子自己被判刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年遭当众殴打。新疆退休法官黄云敏至今家属拿不到判决书。他是因异议学者子肃案被关押的黄晓敏兄长。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黄振超：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">广州维权人士、广州白云区平沙村村民，十多年来为了维护自家以及村民的土地权益，利用所学的法律知识，对多个政府机关申请信息公开和行政诉讼而触怒地方贪官，他也因此多次被地方政府实施报复打击。去年，黄振超因为带领村民到北京旅游而被遣返并被行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月底至<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月初，黄振超因为上北京旅游，自己在广州平沙村的出租屋连续几个晚上遭到街道综治办联合十数名公安、特勤人员的滋扰，它们或以消防不合格为由，或以租客不符合租住手续为由，在租客门上贴通知形式勒令搬离。当局此举，对黄振超一家的生活造成极大的困扰和心理恐惧，同时原租客因为恐惧纷纷退租也造成黄振超的经济损失。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日正欲到外地旅游时，遭到广州白云区公安分局以“扰乱公共场所秩序”为由行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天。<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天拘留期满后的<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，该局又以“寻衅滋事罪”之名把黄振超转为刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黄志球：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">她与陆惠平、陆宗并是福建屏南奇案——一家四口<span lang="EN-US">3</span>人被刑事拘留、<span lang="EN-US">1</span>人被强迫失踪的当事人。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日陆惠平的妹妹陆晶发了一条“父母和姐姐无罪”的微博后，屏南县城关派出所公安上门抓人至今未归。本案简介：陆惠平<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，到屏南县古峰镇长汾社区复印承包地确权材料，全程录音显示陆惠平与工作人员双方都很平和，长汾社区副区长挑起事端，突然窜出殴打陆惠平，声称确权材料是国家秘密，不给复印并招来屏南城关派出所公安，拘留了陆惠平。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日拘留十天期满，陆母黄志球到拘留所接陆惠平回家时双双当场被抓捕，同日陆父陆宗并在家被抓捕。一家三口被以涉嫌“敲诈勒索罪”刑拘。然而，屏南当局对陆家征地分文未补，陆父在征地现场被打断肋骨，陆母气绝服农药险酿命案，该案至今未处理。普通百姓敲诈强大的政府，这逻辑相当怪异。此案于是<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，罪名摇身一变“破坏生产经营罪”，并于<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日执行逮捕，陆惠平和母亲黄志球羁押在宁德看守所，陆父陆宗并羁押在屏南看守所。全家三口被刑拘后，屏南古峰镇政府被福州中院认定“强占土地违法”的情况下，再次开工。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，“福建屏南奇案”陆惠平一家三口被“破坏生产经营罪”一审在屏南法院第二法庭公开宣判，黄志球被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个月，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 22.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">I</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 22.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">．<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 22.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">J</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 22.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">．<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">季孝龙、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">嵇书龙、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吉白（藏）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吉力利•阿布都拉（哈萨克）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">贾国玺、贾灵娟、贾瑞平、贾艳玲、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">嘉扬多吉（藏）、嘉央洛追（藏）、加尔肯别克·卡生巴依（哈）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">江荣欣、<span
